   </h1>

     <p>
      The
      <b>
       Embraer EMB 314 Super Tucano
      </b>
      (
      <span class="unicode haudio" style="white-space:nowrap;">
       <span class="fn">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Tucano_Pronunciation.ogg" title="About this sound">
         <img alt="About this sound" data-file-height="20" data-file-width="20" height="11" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/11px-Loudspeaker.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/17px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/22px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 2x" width="11"/>
        </a>
        <a class="internal" href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b0/Tucano_Pronunciation.ogg" title="Tucano Pronunciation.ogg">
         pronunciation
        </a>
       </span>
      </span>
      ), also named
      <b>
       ALX
      </b>
      or
      <b>
       A-29
      </b>
      is a
      <a href="/wiki/Turboprop" title="Turboprop">
       turboprop
      </a>
      <a href="/wiki/Aircraft" title="Aircraft">
       aircraft
      </a>
      designed for light attack,
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Counter_insurgency" title="Counter insurgency">
       counter insurgency
      </a>
      (
      <a href="/wiki/Counter-insurgency_aircraft" title="Counter-insurgency aircraft">
       COIN
      </a>
      ),
      <a href="/wiki/Close_air_support" title="Close air support">
       close air support
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Aerial_reconnaissance" title="Aerial reconnaissance">
       aerial reconnaissance
      </a>
      missions in low threat environments, as well as providing pilot training. Designed to operate in high temperature and humidity conditions in extremely rugged terrain, the Super Tucano is highly maneuverable, has a low heat signature, incorporates 4th generation
      <a href="/wiki/Avionics" title="Avionics">
       avionics
      </a>
      and weapons system to deliver precision guided munitions. It is currently in service with the
      <a href="/wiki/Air_force" title="Air force">
       air forces
      </a>
      of
      <a href="/wiki/National_Air_Force_of_Angola" title="National Air Force of Angola">
       Angola
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_Air_Force" title="Brazilian Air Force">
       Brazil
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Air_Force" title="Dominican Air Force">
       Dominican Republic
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Colombian_Air_Force" title="Colombian Air Force">
       Colombia
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Ecuadorian_Air_Force" title="Ecuadorian Air Force">
       Ecuador
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Chilean_Air_Force" title="Chilean Air Force">
       Chile
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Military_of_Burkina_Faso" title="Military of Burkina Faso">
       Burkina Faso
      </a>
      ,
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mauritanian_Air_Force" title="Mauritanian Air Force">
       Mauritania
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Indonesian_Air_Force" title="Indonesian Air Force">
       Indonesia
      </a>
      , and the
      <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force" title="United States Air Force">
       United States Air Force
      </a>
      , and has been ordered by
      <a href="/wiki/Senegalese_Air_Force" title="Senegalese Air Force">
       Senegal
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Honduran_Air_Force" title="Honduran Air Force">
       Honduras
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Military_of_Mali#Mali_Air_Force" title="Military of Mali">
       Mali
      </a>
      and Ghana.
     </p>
     <p>
     </p>

     <p>
